# Historical Artifacts Creation #

set_artifact_rarity_common = {
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = quality
		value = 15
	}
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = wealth
		value = 15
	}
}

set_artifact_rarity_masterwork = {
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = quality
		value = 30
	}
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = wealth
		value = 30
	}
}

set_artifact_rarity_famed = {
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = quality
		value = 70
	}
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = wealth
		value = 70
	}
}

set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = {
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = quality
		value = 100
	}
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = wealth
		value = 100
	}
}



### RINGS OF POWER ###

## One Ring

create_artifact_one_ring_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = one_ring_name
		description = one_ring_description
		creator = character:lineofsauron #Sauron
		type = miscellaneous
		visuals = one_ring
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		template = one_ring_template # Template is where you set restrictions on usability!
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 2192.1.1
			actor = character:lineofsauron #Sauron
			recipient = character:lineofsauron #Sauron
			location = province:621 #Orodruin
		}
		modifier = one_ring_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = one_ring
		set_variable = ring_of_power 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Isildur takes the Ring for himself
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = won_in_duel
			DATE = 4033.7.12
			RECIPIENT = character:lineisildur0 #Isildur
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history_location = { # Déagol finds the Ring
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = discovered
			DATE = 6496.5.10
			LOCATION = province:776 #Gladden Fields
			ACTOR = character:lineofgollum5 #Déagol
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofgollum5 #Déagol
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Sméagol takes the Ring from Déagol
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = stolen
			DATE = 6496.5.10
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofgollum3 #Sméagol
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Bilbo Baggins wins the Ring in a game of riddles
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = won_in_duel
			DATE = 6974.6.25
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofbaggins12 #Bilbo Baggins
		}
	}
}


## Elven Rings

create_artifact_nenya_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = nenya_name
		description = nenya_description
		creator = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
		type = miscellaneous
		visuals = nenya
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		template = elven_ring_template # Template is where you set restrictions on usability!
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 2182.1.1
			actor = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
			recipient = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
			location = province:4351 #Ost-in-Edhil
		}
		modifier = nenya_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = nenya
		set_variable = elven_ring
		set_variable = ring_of_power 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Celebrimbor gives Nenya to Galadriel
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 2285.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:linefinwe36 #Galadriel
		}
	}
}

	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = vilya_name
		description = vilya_description
		creator = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
		type = miscellaneous
		visuals = vilya
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		template = elven_ring_template # Template is where you set restrictions on usability!
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 2182.1.1
			actor = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
			recipient = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
			location = province:4351 #Ost-in-Edhil
		}
		modifier = vilya_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = vilya
		set_variable = elven_ring
		set_variable = ring_of_power 
		save_scope_as = epic
		equip_artifact_to_owner = yes


		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Celebrimbor gives Narya to Gil-galad
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 2285.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:linefinwe41 #Gil-galad
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Gil-galad gives Vilya to Elrond
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 2293.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:linefinwe27 #Elrond
		}
	}
}

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = ring_of_longbeards_name
		description = ring_of_dwarves_description
		creator = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
		type = miscellaneous
		visuals = ring_of_longbeards
		wealth = scope:wealth

## Rings of Men

create_artifact_ring_of_men_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = ring_of_men_name
		description = ring_of_men_description
		creator = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
		type = miscellaneous
		visuals = ring_of_men
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		template = ring_of_mortals_template # Template is where you set restrictions on usability!
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 2182.1.1
			actor = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
			recipient = character:linefinwe18  #Celebrimbor
			location = province:4351 #Ost-in-Edhil
		}
		modifier = ring_of_mortals_nazgul_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = ring_of_men
		set_variable = ring_of_mortals
		set_variable = corrupted_ring
		set_variable = ring_of_power
		equip_artifact_to_owner = yes 
		save_scope_as = epic
	}
}

		name = sword_of_manwe_name

		creator = character:lineofeonwe #Eonwe
		type = sword
		visuals = hyandolire
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 1.1.1
			actor = character:lineofeonwe #Eonwe
			recipient = character:lineofeonwe #Eonwe
			location = province:3900 #Valinor
		}
		modifier = sword_of_manwe_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {

		set_variable = sword_of_manwe 
		save_scope_as = epic
	}
}

	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_masterwork = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = ring_saruman_name
		description = ring_saruman_description
		creator = character:lineofsaruman #Saruman
		type = miscellaneous
		visuals = ring
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 6999.1.1
			actor = character:lineofsaruman #Saruman
			recipient = character:lineofsaruman #Saruman
			location = province:20 #Orthanc
		}
		modifier = ring_saruman_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = ring_saruman 
		save_scope_as = epic
	}
}

	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = glamdring_name
		description = {
			desc = glamdring_description
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 6974.5.1 }
				desc = glamdring_description_gandalf
			}
		}
		type = sword
		visuals = glamdring
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 118.1.1
			recipient = character:linefinwe21 #Turgon
		}
		modifier = glamdring_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = glamdring
		set_variable = elven
		set_variable = relic
		equip_artifact_to_owner = yes 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history_location = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = discovered
			DATE = 6974.5.1
			LOCATION = province:4469 #Ettenmoors
			ACTOR = character:lineofbaggins12 # Bilbo Baggins
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofgandalf
		}
	}
}

## Palantir ##

create_artifact_palantir_orthanc_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = palantir_orthanc_name
		description = {
			desc = palantir_description
			desc = palantir_orthanc_description
		}
		type = pedestal
		visuals = palantir
		creator = character:linefinwe2 #Fëanor
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 2.2.1
			actor = character:linefinwe2 #Fëanor
			recipient = character:linefinwe2 #Fëanor
			location = province:3900 #Tirion
		}
		modifier = palantir_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = palantir_orthanc
		set_variable = palantir 
		save_scope_as = epic

		add_artifact_title_history = {
			target = title:e_arnor
			date = 3912.1.1
		}
		add_artifact_title_history = {
			target = title:e_gondor
			date = 3912.1.2
		}
		add_artifact_title_history = {
			target = title:d_isengard
			date = 5200.1.1
		}
	}
}

	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }

	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = palantir_amonsul_name
		description = {
			desc = palantir_description
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 6008.1.1 }
				desc = palantir_amonsul_description
			}
		}
		creator = character:linefinwe2 #Fëanor

		quality = scope:quality

create_artifact_palantir_annuminas_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = palantir_annuminas_name
		description = {
			desc = palantir_description
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 6008.1.1 }
				desc = palantir_amonsul_description
			}
		}
		creator = character:linefinwe2 #Fëanor
		type = pedestal
		visuals = palantir
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 2.2.1
			actor = character:linefinwe2 #Fëanor

		type = pedestal
		visuals = galadriel_mirror
		template = galadriel_mirror_template
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 6014.1.1
			actor = character:linefinwe36 #Galadriel
			recipient = character:linefinwe36 #Galadriel
			location = province:3108 #Caras Galadhon
		}
		modifier = galadriel_mirror_modifier

		save_scope_as = epic
	}
}

	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = pearl_of_ereinion_name
		description = pearl_of_ereinion_description
		type = miscellaneous
		visuals = pearl_of_ereinion
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = discovered
			date = 684.12.2
			actor = character:linefinwe41 #Gil-Galad
			recipient = character:lineofcirdan #Cirdan
			location = province:4266 #Mithlond
		}
		modifier = pearl_of_ereinion_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = pearl_of_ereinion
		set_variable = elven
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic
	}
}

create_artifact_aeglos_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }

	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = aeglos_name
		description = {
			desc = aeglos_description
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 4033.7.12 }
				desc = aeglos_description_thirdage
			}
		}
		type = spear
		visuals = aeglos
		template = hadhafang_template
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 495.1.1
			recipient = character:linefinwe41 #Gil-Galad
		}
		modifier = aeglos_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = aeglos
		set_variable = elven 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Elrond recovers Aeglos from Gil-galad's body
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 4033.7.12
			RECIPIENT = character:linefinwe27 #Elrond
		}
	}
}

create_artifact_arkenstone_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = arkenstone_name
		description = arkenstone_description
		type = pedestal
		visuals = arkenstone
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		template = arkenstone_template
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 6032.1.1
			recipient = character:lineofdurin74
			location = province:4408 #Throne of Erebor
		}
		modifier = arkenstone_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = arkenstone
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic

		if = {
			limit = { game_start_date > 6974.11.30 } #Death of Thorin
			add_artifact_modifier = arkenstone_thorin_modifier
			set_variable = thorins_tomb
		}

		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Thorin I
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 6223.12.25
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofdurin75
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Glóin
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 6322.5.21
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofdurin76
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Óin
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 6418.6.2
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofdurin77
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Náin II
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 6521.3.30
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofdurin78
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Dáin I
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 6618.1.8
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofdurin79
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Thror I
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 6622.1.6
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofdurin81
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history_location = { # Bilbo
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = discovered
			DATE = 6974.10.21
			LOCATION = province:4408 #Throne of Erebor
			ACTOR = character:lineofbaggins12
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofbaggins12
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Bard I of Dale
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 6974.10.25
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofdale46
		}

create_artifact_orcrist_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = orcrist_name
		description = {
			desc = orcrist_description
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 6974.5.1 }
				desc = orcrist_description_thorin
			}
		}
		type = sword
		visuals = orcrist
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 118.1.1
			recipient = character:linefinwe21 #Turgon
		}
		modifier = orcrist_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = orcrist
		set_variable = elven
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic
		
		if = {
			limit = { game_start_date > 6974.11.30 } #Death of Thorin
			add_artifact_modifier = orcrist_thorin_modifier
			set_variable = thorins_tomb
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history_location = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = discovered
			DATE = 6974.5.1
			LOCATION = province:4469 #Ettenmoors
			ACTOR = character:lineofbaggins12 # Bilbo Baggins
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofdurin83 # Thorin II Oakenshield
		}
	}
}

create_artifact_trusty_boots_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_famed = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = trusty_boots_name
		description = trusty_boots_description
		type = miscellaneous
		visuals = trusty_boots
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 6850.1.1
			actor = character:lineofargan1 # The Dad That Walks
			recipient = character:lineofargan2 # The Axe That Walks
			location = province:5052 # Nurt Hanad
		}
		modifier = trusty_boots_modifier
		template = trusty_boots_template
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = trusty_boots
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic
	}
}

# Hobbitses #

create_artifact_sting_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = sting_name
		description = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date < 6974.5.1 }
				desc = sting_description_preBilbo
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date >= 6974.5.1 }
				desc = sting_description_Bilbo
			}
		} 
		type = dagger
		visuals = sting
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 118.1.1
			recipient = character:linefinwe21 #Turgon
		}
		modifier = sting_modifier
		template = sting_template
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = sting
		set_variable = elven
		equip_artifact_to_owner = yes 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history_location = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = discovered
			DATE = 6974.5.1
			LOCATION = province:4469 #Ettenmoors
			ACTOR = character:lineofbaggins12 # Bilbo Baggins
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofbaggins12 # Bilbo Baggins
		}
	}
}

		type = pedestal
		visuals = skull_earnur
		template = skull_earnur_template
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality

create_artifact_throne_of_gondor_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = throne_of_gondor_name
		description = {
			desc = throne_of_gondor_description
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 5480.8.22 }
				desc = throne_of_gondor_description_kinstrife
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 6083.1.1 }
				desc = throne_of_gondor_description_stewards
			}
		}
		type = throne_special
		visuals = throne_of_gondor
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		template = throne_of_gondor_template # Template is where you set restrictions on usability!
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 3912.1.1
			recipient = character:lineofanarion1 # Anarion
			location = province:202 #Osgiliath
		}
		modifier = throne_of_gondor_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = throne_of_gondor
		set_variable = {
			name = artifact_succession_title
			value = title:e_gondor
		}
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 4035.10.5
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofanarion5 # Meneldil

create_artifact_ring_barahir_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = ring_barahir_name
		description = ring_barahir_description
		type = miscellaneous
		template = ring_barahir_template
		visuals = ring_barahir
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 2.1.1
			recipient = character:linefinwe6 # Finarfin
			location = province:3900 # Tirion
		}
		modifier = ring_barahir_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = ring_barahir
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic
		
		if = {
			limit = { exists = title:e_arnor.holder }
			set_variable = {
				name = artifact_succession_title
				value = title:e_arnor
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { exists = title:k_arthedain.holder }
			set_variable = {
				name = artifact_succession_title
				value = title:k_arthedain
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { exists = title:d_northern_dunedain.holder }
			set_variable = {
				name = artifact_succession_title
				value = title:d_northern_dunedain
			}
		}

		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 2.1.2
			RECIPIENT = character:linefinwe33 #Finrod
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {

create_artifact_shards_of_narsil_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = shards_of_narsil_name
		description = shards_of_narsil_description
		creator = character:lineofelwe3 #Thingol
		type = miscellaneous
		visuals = shards_of_narsil
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 262.1.1
			actor = character:lineoftelchar1  #Telchar
			recipient = character:lineofelwe3 #Thingol
			location = province:4869 #Nogrod
		}
		modifier = shards_of_narsil_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = shards_of_narsil
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic
		
		if = {
			limit = { exists = title:e_arnor.holder }
			set_variable = {
				name = artifact_succession_title
				value = title:e_arnor
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { exists = title:k_arthedain.holder }
			set_variable = {
				name = artifact_succession_title
				value = title:k_arthedain
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { exists = title:d_northern_dunedain.holder }
			set_variable = {
				name = artifact_succession_title
				value = title:d_northern_dunedain
			}
		}

		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 504.5.4
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofelwe5 # Dior Eluchil
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 508.2.6
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofelwe9 # Nimloth
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 542.9.10
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofelros1 #Elros
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this

			RECIPIENT = character:lineofelros4 # Elendil
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 1189.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofelros29 #Silmariën
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 1534.1.1

create_artifact_narsil_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = narsil_name
		description = narsil_description
		creator = character:linefinwe27 #Elrond
		type = sword
		visuals = narsil
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 2.1.1
			recipient = character:lineofelwe3 #Thingol
		}
		modifier = narsil_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = narsil
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 504.5.4
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofelwe5 # Dior Eluchil
		}

create_artifact_sceptre_of_annuminas_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = sceptre_of_annuminas_name
		description = {
			desc = sceptre_of_annuminas_description
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 4894.7.12 }
				desc = sceptre_of_annuminas_description_secession
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 6008.12.24 }
				desc = sceptre_of_annuminas_description_fall
			}
		}
		creator = character:lineofelatan2 #Valandil
		type = regalia
		visuals = sceptre_of_annuminas
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 1290.1.1
			recipient = character:lineofelatan2 # Valandil
		}
		modifier = sceptre_of_annuminas_modifier
		template = sceptre_of_annuminas_template
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = sceptre_of_annuminas
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic
		set_variable = {
			name = artifact_succession_title

create_artifact_elendilmir_valandil_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = elendilmir_valandil_name
		description = {
			desc = elendilmir_valandil_description
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 4894.7.12 }
				desc = elendilmir_valandil_description_secession
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 6008.12.24 }
				desc = elendilmir_valandil_description_fall
			}
		}
		creator = character:lineisildur4 #Valandil
		type = helmet
		visuals = elendilmir
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 4035.10.5
			recipient = character:lineisildur4 #Valandil
		}
		modifier = elendilmir_valandil_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = elendilmir_valandil
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic
		set_variable = {
			name = artifact_succession_title
			value = title:e_arnor
		}

		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Eldacar
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 4282.9.29
			RECIPIENT = character:lineisildur5
		}

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {

		type = sword
		visuals = dunachar
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 3792.1.1
			recipient = character:linefinwe27 #Elrond
			location = province:4351 #Ost-in-Edhil
		}
		modifier = dunachar_modifier

		decaying = no

create_artifact_herugrim_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = herugrim_name
		description = herugrim_description
		type = sword
		visuals = herugrim
		template = rohan_royal_weapon_artifact
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 6792.1.1
			recipient = character:lineofeorl16 #Fréaláf
			location = province:1 #Edoras
		}
		modifier = herugrim_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = herugrim
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic

		add_artifact_title_history = {
			target = title:k_rohan
			date = 6792.1.1
		}
	}
}

create_artifact_telperion_chalice_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = telperion_chalice_name
		description = {
			desc = telperion_chalice_description
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 4025.1.1 }
				desc = telperion_chalice_description_oropher
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = { game_start_date > 6791.5.21 }
				desc = telperion_chalice_description_dorwinion
			}
		}
		type = pedestal
		visuals = telperion_chalice
		template = twin_chalice_template
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 4022.1.1
			recipient = character:linefinwe41 #Gil-Galad
			location = province:4266 #Mithlond
		}
		modifier = twin_chalice_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = telperion_chalice
		set_variable = {
			name = artifact_succession_title
			value = title:k_dorwinion
		}
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Gil-galad gives the chalice to Oropher
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 4025.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:lineoforopher1 #Oropher
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 4026.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:lineoforopher3 #Thranduil
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Thranduil sends the twin chalices as a coronation gift
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 6791.5.21
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofkoldana75 #Bladorthin
		}
		add_artifact_title_history = {
			target = title:k_dorwinion
			date = 6839.12.20
		}
	}
}

## Rhûn and Khand ##

create_artifact_throne_ovatha_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_famed = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = throne_ovatha_name
		description = throne_ovatha_description
		type = throne_special
		visuals = throne
		template = throne_ovatha_template
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 6950.1.1
			recipient = character:lineofkeiseimu2 #Ôvatha IX
			location = province:2446 #Starlustsa Khand
		}
		modifier = throne_ovatha_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = throne_ovatha
		set_variable = {
			name = artifact_succession_title
			value = title:e_khand
		}
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic

		add_artifact_title_history = {
			target = title:c_madh_ortogh
			date = 6966.6.22
		}
	}
}

	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_famed = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = mundburgian_shield_name
		description = mundburgian_shield_description
		type = brooch
		visuals = mundburgian_shield
		template = general_unique_template
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		modifier = mundburgian_shield_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = yes
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = mundburgian_shield 
		save_scope_as = epic
	}
}

## Adventure Uniques ##

create_artifact_dragon_helm_of_dor_lomin_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = dragon_helm_of_dor_lomin_name
		description = dragon_helm_of_dor_lomin_description
		type = helmet
		visuals = dragon_helm_of_dor_lomin
		template = dragon_helm_of_dor_lomin_template
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 262.1.1
			actor = character:lineoftelchar1  #Telchar
			recipient = character:lineofdwalin5 # Azaghâl
			location = province:4869 #Nogrod
		}
		modifier = dragon_helm_of_dor_lomin_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = dragon_helm_of_dor_lomin
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 83.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:linefinwe10 #Maedhros
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 93.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:linefinwe20 #Fingon
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 419.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofhador1 #Hador
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 457.5.29
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofhador3 #Galdor
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 464.8.18
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofhador5 #Hurin
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 474.2.3
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofbeor24 #Morwen Eledhwen
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 475.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofelwe3 #Elu Thingol
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given
			DATE = 482.9.3
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofhador7 #Turin Turambar etc
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 501.6.12
			RECIPIENT = character:lineofhador5 #Hurin
		}
	}
}

create_artifact_dramborleg_effect = {
	# Get the character the artifact is being made for.
	$OWNER$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_illustrious = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = dramborleg_name
		description = dramborleg_description
		type = axe
		visuals = dramborleg
		template = dramborleg_template
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		history = {
			type = created
			date = 500.1.1
			recipient = character:lineofhador10 #Tuor
		}
		modifier = dramborleg_modifier
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = no
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = dramborleg
		set_variable = elven
		set_variable = relic 
		save_scope_as = epic

		lotr_add_artifact_history = { # Earendil
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = inherited
			DATE = 528.1.1
			RECIPIENT = character:linefinwe26
		}
		lotr_add_artifact_history = {
			ARTIFACT = this
			TYPE = given

	# Not really used, but if we don't set the scopes we get errors in the feature selection
	set_artifact_rarity_famed = yes

	# Create the artifact
	create_artifact = {
		name = crown_of_herumor_name
		description = crown_of_herumor_description
		type = helmet
		visuals = crown
		wealth = scope:wealth
		quality = scope:quality
		modifier = crown_of_bn_modifier
		template = crown_of_bn_template
		save_scope_as = newly_created_artifact
		decaying = yes
	}

	scope:newly_created_artifact = {
		set_variable = { name = historical_unique_artifact value = yes }
		set_variable = crown_of_herumor 
		save_scope_as = epic
	}
}
